If the pod sandbox does not\n98:     // exist, the call returns an error.\n99:     rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n100:     // ListPodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandboxes matching a filter.\n101:     rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n102: \n103:     // UpdateRuntimeConfig updates the runtime configuration based on the given request.\n104:     rpc UpdateRuntimeConfig(UpdateRuntimeConfigRequest) returns (UpdateRuntimeConfigResponse) {}\n105: \n106:     // Status returns the status of the runtime.\n107:     rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse) {}\n108: \n109:     // CheckpointContainer checkpoints a container\n110:     rpc CheckpointContainer(CheckpointContainerRequest) returns (CheckpointContainerResponse) {}\n111: \n112:     // GetContainerEvents gets container events from the CRI runtime\n113:     rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse) {}\n114: \n115:     // ListMetricDescriptors gets the descriptors for the metrics that will be returned in ListPodSandboxMetrics.\n116:     // This list should be static at startup: either the client and server restart together when\n117:     // adding or removing metrics descriptors, or they should not change.\n118:     // Put differently, if ListPodSandboxMetrics references a name that is not described in the initial\n119:     // ListMetricDescriptors call, then the metric will not be broadcasted.\n120:     rpc ListMetricDescriptors(ListMetricDescriptorsRequest) returns (ListMetricDescriptorsResponse) {}\n121: \n122:     // ListPodSandboxMetrics gets pod sandbox metrics from CRI Runtime\n123:     rpc ListPodSandboxMetrics(ListPodSandboxMetricsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxMetricsResponse) {}\n124: \n125:     // RuntimeConfig returns configuration information of the runtime.\n126:     // A couple of notes:\n127:     // - The RuntimeConfigRequest object is not to be confused with the contents of UpdateRuntimeConfigRequest.\n128:     //   The former is for having runtime tell Kubelet what to do, the latter vice versa.\n129:     // - It is the expectation of the Kubelet that these fields are static for the lifecycle of the Kubelet.\n130:     //   The Kubelet will not re-request the RuntimeConfiguration after startup, and CRI implementations should\n131:     //   avoid updating them without a full node reboot.\n132:     rpc RuntimeConfig(RuntimeConfigRequest) returns (RuntimeConfigResponse) {}\n133: \n134:     // UpdatePodSandboxResources synchronously updates the PodSandboxConfig with\n135:     // the pod-level resource configuration. This method is called _after_ the\n136:     // Kubelet reconfigures the pod-level cgroups.\n137:     // This request is treated as best effort, and failure will not block the\n138:     // Kubelet with proceeding with a resize.\n139:     rpc UpdatePodSandboxResources(UpdatePodSandboxResourcesRequest) returns (UpdatePodSandboxResourcesResponse) {}\n140: }\n141: \n142: // ImageService defines the public APIs for managing images.\n143: service ImageService {\n144:     // ListImages lists existing images.\n145:     rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n146:     // ImageStatus returns the status of the image. If the image is not\n147:     // present, returns a response with ImageStatusResponse.Image set to\n148:     // nil.\n149:     rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n150:     // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n151:     rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n152:     // RemoveImage removes the image.\n153:     // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the image has\n154:     // already been removed.\n155:     // Note that if the image is referenced by multiple tags (even across different repositories\n156:     // if they resolve to the same image digest), removing the image by a single tag\n157:     // will remove all of its tags. For example, if `repo/image:v1` and `another_repo/image:latest`\n158:     // point to the same image, removing `repo/image:v1` will also remove `another_repo/image:latest`.\n159:     // The next call to ListImages, ImageStatus, ImageFsInfo will not return this image.\n160:     // The resources (e.g. disk space) may be cleaned asynchronously\n161:     // and not guaranteed to be cleaned up by the time this method returns.\n162:     rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n163:     // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n164:     // Usage information may include images that were removed, but are still being cleaned up.\n165:     rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n166: }\n167: \n168: message VersionRequest {\n169:     // Version of the kubelet runtime API.\n170:     string version = 1;\n171: }\n172: \n173: message VersionResponse {\n174:     // Version of the kubelet runtime API.\n175:     string version = 1;\n176:     // Name of the container runtime.\n177:     string runtime_name = 2;\n178:     // Version of the container runtime. Default: 0 (not specified).\n208:     int32 container_port = 2;\n209:     // Port number on the host to map the container port to.\n210:     //\n211:     // * Valid host port range is 1-65535.\n212:     // * The value 0 has explicit semantic meaning: it indicates NO host port should be allocated.\n213:     // * The value 0 does NOT indicate dynamic port allocation. Future implementations\n214:     //   of dynamic allocation will use different values/semantics.\n215:     // * Implementations MUST handle the case where this field is explicitly set to 0,\n216:     //   This field SHOULD be omitted when no port is required.\n217:     //\n218:     // Default: If omitted, container port will not be exposed on the host.\n219:     int32 host_port = 3;\n220:     // Host IP.\n221:     string host_ip = 4;\n222: }\n223: \n224: enum MountPropagation {\n225:     // No mount propagation (\"rprivate\" in Linux terminology).\n226:     PROPAGATION_PRIVATE = 0;\n227:     // Mounts get propagated from the host to the container (\"rslave\" in Linux).\n228:     PROPAGATION_HOST_TO_CONTAINER = 1;\n229:     // Mounts get propagated from the host to the container and from the\n230:     // container to the host (\"rshared\" in Linux).\n231:     PROPAGATION_BIDIRECTIONAL = 2;\n232: }\n233: \n234: // Mount specifies a host volume to mount into a container.\n235: message Mount {\n236:     // Path of the mount within the container.\n237:     string container_path = 1;\n238:     // Path of the mount on the host. Has to be empty if the image field below\n239:     // is provided, because those fields are mutually exclusive. If the image\n240:     // field below is nil and the host path doesn't exist, then runtimes should\n241:     // report an error. If the hostpath is a symbolic link, runtimes should\n242:     // follow the symlink and mount the real destination to container.\n243:     string host_path = 2;\n244:     // If set, the mount is read-only.\n245:     bool readonly = 3;\n246:     // If set, the mount needs SELinux relabeling.\n247:     bool selinux_relabel = 4;\n248:     // Requested propagation mode.\n249:     MountPropagation propagation = 5;\n250:     // UidMappings specifies the runtime UID mappings for the mount.\n251:     repeated IDMapping uidMappings = 6;\n252:     // GidMappings specifies the runtime GID mappings for the mount.\n253:     repeated IDMapping gidMappings = 7;\n254:     // If set to true, the mount is made recursive read-only.\n255:     // In this CRI API, recursive_read_only is a plain true/false boolean, although its equivalent\n256:     // in the Kubernetes core API is a quaternary that can be nil, \"Enabled\", \"IfPossible\", or \"Disabled\".\n257:     // kubelet translates that quaternary value in the core API into a boolean in this CRI API.\n258:     // Remarks:\n259:     // - nil is just treated as false\n260:     // - when set to true, readonly must be explicitly set to true, and propagation must be PRIVATE (0).\n261:     // - (readonly == false && recursive_read_only == false) does not make the mount read-only.\n262:     bool recursive_read_only = 8;\n263:     // Mount an image reference (image ID, with or without digest), which is a\n264:     // special use case for image volume mounts. If this field is set, then\n265:     // host_path should be unset. All image mounts are per feature definition\n266:     // readonly (noexec). The kubelet does an PullImage RPC and evaluates the returned\n267:     // PullImageResponse.image_ref value, which is then set to the\n268:     // ImageSpec.image field. Runtimes are expected to mount the image as\n269:     // required.\n270:     // Introduced in the Image Volume Source KEP: https://kep.k8s.io/4639\n271:     ImageSpec image = 9;\n272:     // Specific image sub path to be used from inside the image instead of its\n273:     // root, only necessary if the above image field is set. If the sub path is\n274:     // not empty and does not exist in the image, then runtimes should fail and\n275:     // return an error.\n276:     // Introduced in the Image Volume Source KEP beta graduation: https://kep.k8s.io/4639\n277:     string image_sub_path = 10;\n278: }\n279: \n280: // IDMapping describes host to container ID mappings for a pod sandbox.\n281: message IDMapping {\n282:     // HostId is the id on the host.\n283:     uint32 host_id = 1;\n284:     // ContainerId is the id in the container.\n285:     uint32 container_id = 2;\n286:     // Length is the size of the range to map.\n287:     uint32 length = 3;\n288: }\n289: \n290: // A NamespaceMode describes the intended namespace configuration for each\n291: // of the namespaces (Network, PID, IPC) in NamespaceOption. Runtimes should\n292: // map these modes as appropriate for the technology underlying the runtime.\n293: enum NamespaceMode {\n294:     // A POD namespace is common to all containers in a pod.\n295:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of POD expects to view\n296:     // all of the processes in all of the containers in the pod.\n297:     POD       = 0;\n298:     // A CONTAINER namespace is restricted to a single container.\n299:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of CONTAINER expects to\n300:     // view only the processes in that container.\n301:     CONTAINER = 1;\n302:     // A NODE namespace is the namespace of the Kubernetes node.\n303:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of NODE expects to view\n304:     // all of the processes on the host running the kubelet.\n305:     NODE      = 2;\n306:     // TARGET targets the namespace of another container. When this is specified,\n307:     // a target_id must be specified in NamespaceOption and refer to a container\n308:     // previously created with NamespaceMode CONTAINER. This containers namespace\n309:     // will be made to match that of container target_id.\n310:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of TARGET expects to view\n311:     // all of the processes that container target_id can view.\n312:     TARGET    = 3;\n313: }\n314: \n315: // UserNamespace describes the intended user namespace configuration for a pod sandbox.\n316: message UserNamespace {\n317:     // Mode is the NamespaceMode for this UserNamespace.\n318:     // Note: NamespaceMode for UserNamespace currently supports only POD and NODE, not CONTAINER OR TARGET.\n319:     NamespaceMode mode = 1;\n320: \n321:     // Uids specifies the UID mappings for the user namespace.\n322:     repeated IDMapping uids = 2;\n323: \n324:     // Gids specifies the GID mappings for the user namespace.\n325:     repeated IDMapping gids = 3;\n326: }\n327: \n328: // NamespaceOption provides options for Linux namespaces.\n329: message NamespaceOption {\n330:     // Network namespace for this container/sandbox.\n331:     // Note: There is currently no way to set CONTAINER scoped network in the Kubernetes API.\n332:     // Namespaces currently set by the kubelet: POD, NODE\n333:     NamespaceMode network = 1;\n334:     // PID namespace for this container/sandbox.\n335:     // Note: The CRI default is POD, but the v1.PodSpec default is CONTAINER.\n336:     // The kubelet's runtime manager will set this to CONTAINER explicitly for v1 pods.\n337:     // Namespaces currently set by the kubelet: POD, CONTAINER, NODE, TARGET\n338:     NamespaceMode pid = 2;\n339:     // IPC namespace for this container/sandbox.\n340:     // Note: There is currently no way to set CONTAINER scoped IPC in the Kubernetes API.\n341:     // Namespaces currently set by the kubelet: POD, NODE\n342:     NamespaceMode ipc = 3;\n343:     // Target Container ID for NamespaceMode of TARGET. This container must have been\n344:     // previously created in the same pod. It is not possible to specify different targets\n345:     // for each namespace.\n346:     string target_id = 4;\n347:     // UsernsOptions for this pod sandbox.\n348:     // The Kubelet picks the user namespace configuration to use for the pod sandbox.  The mappings\n349:     // are specified as part of the UserNamespace struct.  If the struct is nil, then the POD mode\n350:     // must be assumed.  This is done for backward compatibility with older Kubelet versions that\n351:     // do not set a user namespace.\n352:     UserNamespace userns_options = 5;\n353: }\n354: \n355: // SupplementalGroupsPolicy defines how supplemental groups \n356: // of the first container processes are calculated.\n357: enum SupplementalGroupsPolicy {\n358:     // Merge means that the container's provided SupplementalGroups \n359:     // and FsGroup (specified in SecurityContext) will be merged with \n360:     // the primary user's groups as defined in the container image\n361:     // (in /etc/group).\n362:     Merge = 0;\n363:     // Strict means that the container's provided SupplementalGroups\n364:     // and FsGroup (specified in SecurityContext) will be used instead of \n365:     // any groups defined in the container image.\n366:     Strict = 1;\n367: }\n368: \n369: // Int64Value is the wrapper of int64.\n370: message Int64Value {\n371:     // The value.\n372:     int64 value = 1;\n373: }\n374: \n375: // LinuxSandboxSecurityContext holds linux security configuration that will be\n376: // applied to a sandbox. If a privileged container is to be executed within it, this\n403:     // MUST be true.\n404:     // This allows a sandbox to take additional security precautions if no\n405:     // privileged containers are expected to be run.\n406:     bool privileged = 6;\n407:     // Seccomp profile for the sandbox.\n408:     SecurityProfile seccomp = 9;\n409:     // AppArmor profile for the sandbox.\n410:     SecurityProfile apparmor = 10;\n411:     // Seccomp profile for the sandbox, candidate values are:\n412:     // * runtime/default: the default profile for the container <full-path-to-profile> is the full path of the profile.\n416:     // Default: \"\", which is identical with unconfined.\n417:     string seccomp_profile_path = 7 [deprecated=true];\n418: }\n419: \n420: // A security profile which can be used for sandboxes and containers.\n421: message SecurityProfile {\n422:     // Available profile types.\n423:     enum ProfileType {\n424:         // The However, the LogDirectory may contain\n487:     // binary log files with structured logging data from the individual\n488:     // containers. string type = 3;\n899:     string level = 4;\n900: }\n901: \n902: // Capability contains the container capabilities to add or drop\n903: // Dropping a capability will drop it from all sets.\n904: // applied to a container.\n920: message LinuxContainerSecurityContext {\n921:     // Capabilities to add or drop.\n922:     Capability capabilities = 1;\n923:     // If set, run container in privileged mode.\n924:     // Privileged mode is incompatible with the following options. If any required condition is unmet, the node will be not ready.\n1687: // The required conditions include:\n1688: //   * RuntimeReady: RuntimeReady means the runtime is up and ready to accept\n1689: //   basic containers e.g. container only needs host network.\n1690: //   * NetworkReady: NetworkReady means the runtime network is up and ready to\n1691: //   accept containers which require container network.\n1692: // 2. The analysis spans both the Kubernetes and containerd repositories, mapping the interface contract to concrete implementation.\n\n---\n\n## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition\n\n### 1.1 Definition Location\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n\nThe Kubernetes project maintains the Container Runtime Interface as a protocol buffer specification with gRPC service definitions. This is the source of truth for all container runtime implementations.\n\n### 1.2 Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService\n\nThe CRI RuntimeService gRPC interface defines the following key RPC methods:\n\n#### Sandbox Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\nservice RuntimeService {\n    // Version returns the runtime name, runtime version, and runtime API version.\n    rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse) {}\n\n    // RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes must ensure\n    // the sandbox is in the ready state on success.\n    rpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // StopPodSandbox stops any running process that is part of the sandbox and\n    // reclaims network resources (e.g., IP addresses) allocated to the sandbox.\n    // If there are any running containers in the sandbox, they must be forcibly\n    // terminated. This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if all\n    // relevant resources have already been reclaimed.\n    rpc StopPodSandbox(StopPodSandboxRequest) returns (StopPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox. If there are any running containers\n    // in the sandbox, they must be forcibly terminated and removed.\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the sandbox has\n    // already been removed.\n    rpc RemovePodSandbox(RemovePodSandboxRequest) returns (RemovePodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStatus returns the status of the PodSandbox. If the PodSandbox is\n    // not present, returns an error.\n    rpc PodSandboxStatus(PodSandboxStatusRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandbox returns a list of PodSandboxes.\n    rpc ListPodSandbox(ListPodSandboxRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n#### Container Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\n    // CreateContainer creates a new container in specified PodSandbox\n    rpc CreateContainer(CreateContainerRequest) returns (CreateContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StartContainer starts the container.\n    rpc StartContainer(StartContainerRequest) returns (StartContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StopContainer stops a running container with a grace period (i.e., timeout).\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the container has\n    // already been stopped.\n    rpc StopContainer(StopContainerRequest) returns (StopContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveContainer removes the container. If the container is running, the\n    // container must be forcibly removed.\n    rpc RemoveContainer(RemoveContainerRequest) returns (RemoveContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainers lists all containers by filters.\n    rpc ListContainers(ListContainersRequest) returns (ListContainersResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStatus returns status of the container. If the container is not\n    // present, returns an error.\n    rpc ContainerStatus(ContainerStatusRequest) returns (ContainerStatusResponse) {}\n```\n\n#### Advanced Operations\n```protobuf\n    // ExecSync runs a command in a container synchronously.\n    rpc ExecSync(ExecSyncRequest) returns (ExecSyncResponse) {}\n\n    // Exec prepares a streaming endpoint to execute a command in the container.\n    rpc Exec(ExecRequest) returns (ExecResponse) {}\n\n    // Attach prepares a streaming endpoint to attach to a running container.\n    rpc Attach(AttachRequest) returns (AttachResponse) {}\n\n    // PortForward prepares a streaming endpoint to forward ports from a PodSandbox.\n    rpc PortForward(PortForwardRequest) returns (PortForwardResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStats returns stats of the container.\n    rpc ContainerStats(ContainerStatsRequest) returns (ContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainerStats returns stats of all running containers.\n    rpc ListContainerStats(ListContainerStatsRequest) returns (ListContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandbox.\n    rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandboxes matching a filter.\n    rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // Status returns the status of the runtime.\n    rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse) {}\n\n    // GetContainerEvents gets container events from the CRI runtime\n    rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse) {}\n```\n\n### 1.3 ImageService gRPC Definition\n\nThe CRI also defines an ImageService interface:\n\n```protobuf\nservice ImageService {\n    // ListImages lists existing images.\n    rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageStatus returns the status of the image. If the image is not present,\n    // returns a response with ImageStatusResponse.Image set to nil.\n    rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n    rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveImage removes the image.\n    rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n    rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Message Type Hierarchy\n\nThe proto definitions include structured message types that form a clear contract:\n\n### Pod Sandbox Messages\n- `RunPodSandboxRequest` / `RunPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Contains `PodSandboxConfig` with metadata, network config, DNS, Linux config, etc.\n  - Returns the sandbox ID as a string\n- `StopPodSandboxRequest` / `StopPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `RemovePodSandboxRequest` / `RemovePodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `PodSandboxStatus` message contains:\n  - Sandbox ID, state, creation timestamp\n  - Network settings, metadata labels\n  - Linux-specific namespace paths\n\n### Container Messages\n- `CreateContainerRequest` / `CreateContainerResponse`\n- `StartContainerRequest` / `StartContainerResponse`\n- `ContainerStatus` contains state (created, running, exited) and detailed resource info\n\n---\n\n## 3. Generated gRPC Code\n\n### 3.1 gRPC Compilation\nThe proto files are compiled to generate:\n- **File**: `api_grpc.pb.go` - Contains the gRPC service definitions\n- Generated client interface: `RuntimeServiceClient`\n- Generated server interface: `RuntimeServiceServer`\n- Method handlers and registration functions\n\n### 3.2 Server Interface Example\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n    PodSandboxStatus(context.Context, *PodSandboxStatusRequest) (*PodSandboxStatusResponse, error)\n    // ... other methods\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Registration Function\n```go\nfunc RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s grpc.ServiceRegistrar, srv RuntimeServiceServer) {\n    // Registers all RPC handlers with the gRPC server\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### 4.1 Entry Point: CRI Plugin Registration\n\n**File**: `plugins/cri/cri.go` (containerd repository)\n\nThe containerd CRI plugin is initialized as a gRPC plugin:\n\n```go\nfunc init() {\n    defaultConfig := criconfig.DefaultServerConfig()\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,      // Runtime service\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,      // Sandbox controller\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,          // Node Resource Interface\n            plugins.EventPlugin,\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,\n        },\n        InitFn: initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 gRPC Server Implementation\n\n**Type**: `criGRPCServer` struct\n\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Embedded interface implementation\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer    // Embedded interface implementation\n    io.Closer\n    initializer                   // IsInitialized() method\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nThis structure:\n- **Embeds** the gRPC server interfaces from the CRI API\n- **Wraps** them with instrumentation for logging, metrics, and tracing\n- **Registers** both services with the gRPC server\n\n### 4.3 Service Implementation Layer\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe actual implementation is in the `criService` struct:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    RuntimeService    // Embedded dependency\n    ImageService      // Embedded dependency\n\n    // State management\n    config             criconfig.Config\n    sandboxStore       *sandboxstore.Store    // Stores pod sandbox metadata\n    containerStore     *containerstore.Store  // Stores container metadata\n    sandboxNameIndex   *registrar.Registrar   // Ensures unique names\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n\n    // Network and streaming\n    netPlugin          map[string]cni.CNI    // CNI plugin for networking\n    streamServer       streaming.Server      // For exec/attach streams\n\n    // Monitoring and integration\n    eventMonitor       *events.EventMonitor  // Container event tracking\n    nri                *nri.API              // Node Resource Interface\n    sandboxService     sandboxService        // Sandbox controller\n    runtimeHandlers    map[string]*runtime.RuntimeHandler\n    statsCollector     *StatsCollector\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 Method Implementation Example: RunPodSandbox\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and reserve name to prevent concurrent creation\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    metadata := config.GetMetadata()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n\n    if err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name: %w\", err)\n    }\n    defer func() {\n        if retErr != nil {\n            c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(name)\n        }\n    }()\n\n    // 2. Create lease for resource tracking\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    ls, err := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create lease: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Select OCI runtime based on config and runtime handler\n    ociRuntime, err := c.config.GetSandboxRuntime(config, r.GetRuntimeHandler())\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to get OCI runtime: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 4. Create sandbox store entry\n    sandbox := sandboxstore.NewSandbox(\n        sandboxstore.Metadata{\n            ID:             id,\n            Name:           name,\n            Config:         config,\n            RuntimeHandler: r.GetRuntimeHandler(),\n        },\n        sandboxstore.Status{\n            State: sandboxstore.StateUnknown,\n        },\n    )\n\n    // 5. Set up networking (CNI)\n    // 6. Start the sandbox via sandbox controller\n    // 7. Trigger NRI hooks for Node Resource Interface\n\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{\n        PodSandboxId: id,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Patterns:\n- **Resource isolation**: Each sandbox gets a lease for resource cleanup\n- **Name reservation**: Prevents concurrent creation of same sandbox\n- **Store management**: Maintains metadata in `sandboxStore` for lifecycle tracking\n- **Error recovery**: Deferred cleanup functions ensure partial failures are rolled back\n- **Instrumentation**: Wrapped with tracing spans and logging\n\n### 4.5 StopPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Look up sandbox in store (idempotent - returns success if not found)\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            // Idempotent: already stopped/removed, return success\n            return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error finding sandbox: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 2. Stop all containers in the sandbox (forced termination)\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.stopContainerRetryOnConnectionClosed(ctx, container, 0); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Stop the sandbox container itself if running or unknown\n    state := sandbox.Status.Get().State\n    if state == sandboxstore.StateReady || state == sandboxstore.StateUnknown {\n        if err := c.sandboxService.StopSandbox(ctx, sandbox.Sandboxer, sandbox.ID); err != nil {\n            if !errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop sandbox: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 4. Trigger NRI hooks\n    // 5. Update sandbox state to \"NotReady\"\n\n    return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Points:\n- **Idempotent semantics**: Returns success even if sandbox already stopped\n- **Cascading shutdown**: Stops all containers first, then the sandbox\n- **State tracking**: Uses internal state to avoid redundant operations\n- **Error handling**: Distinguishes between \"not found\" (ok) and real errors\n\n### 4.6 RemovePodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Find the sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // 2. Force-remove all containers in the sandbox\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.removeContainer(ctx, container.ID); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to remove container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Trigger NRI removal hooks\n    // 4. Release the sandbox name from the index\n    // 5. Delete lease\n    // 6. Remove from sandbox store\n\n    return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Instrumentation Layer\n\n### 5.1 Middleware Pattern\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\nContainerd wraps the criService with an instrumented service that adds:\n\n```go\ntype instrumentedService struct {\n    c runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Wrapped service\n}\n\nfunc (in *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Check if service is initialized\n    if err := in.checkInitialized(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // Log the request\n    log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox for %+v\", r.GetConfig().GetMetadata())\n\n    // Call the actual implementation\n    res, err := in.c.RunPodSandbox(ctx, r)\n\n    // Log the response or error\n    if err != nil {\n        log.G(ctx).WithError(err).Errorf(\"RunPodSandbox failed\")\n    } else {\n        log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox returns sandbox id %q\", res.GetPodSandboxId())\n    }\n\n    return res, err\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern provides:\n- **Logging**: Detailed request/response logging\n- **Metrics**: Request timing and counts\n- **Tracing**: Distributed tracing spans\n- **Validation**: Server initialization checks\n\n---\n\n## 6. Kubernetes Vendoring of Containerd APIs\n\n### 6.1 Vendor Structure\n\n**Location**: `vendor/github.com/containerd/` (in kubernetes repo)\n\nKubernetes vendors only the **API types** from containerd, not the full implementation:\n\n```\nvendor/github.com/containerd/\n├── containerd/\n│   └── api/\n│       ├── services/      # gRPC service definitions\n│       └── types/         # Common data types\n├── errdefs/              # Error definitions\n├── log/                  # Logging interface\n├── ttrpc/               # ttrpc protocol implementation\n└── typeurl/             # Type URL registry for protobuf\n```\n\n### 6.2 Key Vendored Components\n\n**containerd/api/types**: Core container and sandbox types that represent the container runtime state\n\n**containerd/errdefs**: Error codes that containerd uses:\n- `IsNotFound(err)` - checks if resource doesn't exist\n- `IsAlreadyExists(err)` - resource creation collision\n- `IsInvalidArgument(err)` - malformed request\n- `IsFailedPrecondition(err)` - resource in wrong state\n\nThis error package is critical for the idempotent semantics of CRI operations.\n\n### 6.3 Kubernetes CRI Client\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`\n\nKubernetes implements a client that communicates with containerd via the CRI interface:\n\n```go\ntype remoteRuntimeService struct {\n    runtimeClient runtimeapi.RuntimeServiceClient  // gRPC client\n    timeout       time.Duration\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig, runtimeHandler string) (string, error) {\n\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    resp, err := r.runtimeClient.RunPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.RunPodSandboxRequest{\n        Config:         config,\n        RuntimeHandler: runtimeHandler,\n    })\n\n    if err != nil {\n        return \"\", err\n    }\n\n    return resp.PodSandboxId, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, podSandBoxID string) error {\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    _, err := r.runtimeClient.StopPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.StopPodSandboxRequest{\n        PodSandboxId: podSandBoxID,\n    })\n\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Interface Contract and Semantics\n\n### 7.1 Idempotent Operations\n\nBoth `StopPodSandbox` and `RemovePodSandbox` are **idempotent**:\n- Multiple calls with same ID should succeed\n- Calling on non-existent resource should return success\n- Kubelet relies on this for reliable cleanup\n\n**Implementation guarantee**: In both containerd and Kubernetes client:\n```\nif err != nil && !isNotFound(err) {\n    return err\n}\n// Return success regardless\n```\n\n### 7.2 Cascading Lifecycle\n\nThe CRI defines a specific lifecycle:\n1. **RunPodSandbox** - Creates and starts sandbox (must be Ready)\n2. **CreateContainer** - Creates containers in the sandbox\n3. **StartContainer** - Starts the containers\n4. **StopContainer** - Stops containers gracefully\n5. **StopPodSandbox** - Stops sandbox (must terminate all containers)\n6. **RemoveContainer** - Removes container metadata\n7. **RemovePodSandbox** - Removes sandbox metadata\n\nContainerd enforces this through state tracking and cascading cleanup.\n\n### 7.3 Graceful vs Forced Termination\n\n- **StopContainer(grace_period)**: Sends SIGTERM, waits for grace period, then SIGKILL\n- **StopPodSandbox**: Forcibly terminates all containers (grace period = 0)\n- **RemovePodSandbox**: Forcibly removes all containers\n\n### 7.4 Resource Cleanup\n\nThree levels of resource management:\n1. **Leases** (containerd): Automatic cleanup of orphaned resources\n2. **Stores** (criService): In-memory tracking of sandbox/container metadata\n3. **CNI plugins**: Network namespace cleanup on sandbox removal\n\n---\n\n## 8. Message Flow Example: Create and Run Pod\n\n### Complete Request-Response Chain\n\n```\nKubelet Requests:\n1. RunPodSandbox(config)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.RunPodSandbox()\n   → Creates lease, reserves name, creates sandbox store entry\n   → Calls sandboxService.StartSandbox() with OCI runtime\n   → Returns sandbox_id\n   Response: RunPodSandboxResponse { pod_sandbox_id = \"abc123\" }\n\n2. CreateContainer(sandbox_id, config)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.CreateContainer()\n   → Creates container store entry\n   → Generates OCI spec from config\n   Response: CreateContainerResponse { container_id = \"def456\" }\n\n3. StartContainer(container_id)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.StartContainer()\n   → Calls sandboxService.StartTask() to run OCI runtime\n   Response: StartContainerResponse {}\n\n4. PodSandboxStatus(sandbox_id)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.PodSandboxStatus()\n   → Returns sandbox state from store\n   Response: PodSandboxStatusResponse { status = SANDBOX_READY, ... }\n\nLater for cleanup:\n5. StopContainer(container_id, grace_period)\n   → Sends SIGTERM, waits, then SIGKILL\n   Response: StopContainerResponse {}\n\n6. RemoveContainer(container_id)\n   Response: RemoveContainerResponse {}\n\n7. StopPodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   → Stops all containers in sandbox\n   → Stops sandbox container\n   Response: StopPodSandboxResponse {}\n\n8. RemovePodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   → Removes all containers\n   → Releases name reservation\n   → Deletes lease\n   → Removes from store\n   Response: RemovePodSandboxResponse {}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Error Handling\n\n### 9.1 Error Types from Kubernetes CRI Spec\n\nAll operations return gRPC errors that map to error codes:\n- `Unimplemented` - Method not supported\n- `Internal` - Unexpected runtime error\n- `InvalidArgument` - Bad request parameters\n- `AlreadyExists` - Resource already created\n- `NotFound` - Resource doesn't exist\n- `FailedPrecondition` - Resource in wrong state\n\n### 9.2 Idempotency Handling\n\nContainerd's idempotent error handling:\n```go\n// In StopPodSandbox\nsandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(id)\nif err != nil {\n    if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n        return &StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil  // Success even if not found\n    }\n    return nil, err  // Real error\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Architecture Summary\n\n### 10.1 Layered Design\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ Kubernetes kubelet                              │\n│ (CRI client - runtime.RuntimeServiceClient)     │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │ gRPC calls over Unix socket\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ Containerd CRI Plugin (plugins/cri/cri.go)      │\n│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐   │\n│ │ criGRPCServer                            │   │\n│ │ - Embeds RuntimeServiceServer            │   │\n│ │ - Embeds ImageServiceServer              │   │\n│ └──────────────────────────────────────────┘   │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ Instrumentation Layer (internal/cri/instrument) │\n│ - Logging, metrics, tracing                     │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ criService Implementation                       │\n│ - sandbox_run.go: RunPodSandbox                 │\n│ - sandbox_stop.go: StopPodSandbox               │\n│ - sandbox_remove.go: RemovePodSandbox           │\n│ - container_*.go: Container operations          │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ Internal Services                               │\n│ - sandboxStore: State management                │\n│ - containerStore: Container tracking            │\n│ - sandboxService: Sandbox controller (runc)    │\n│ - streamServer: Exec/attach streaming           │\n│ - eventMonitor: Container event tracking        │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### 10.2 Key Design Principles\n\n1. **Interface-based abstraction**: CRI defines the contract, containerd implements it\n2. **Idempotent semantics**: Operations can be safely retried\n3. **Resource tracking**: Leases and stores manage resource lifecycle\n4. **State management**: Internal state prevents race conditions\n5. **Instrumentation**: Logging, metrics, and tracing at multiple layers\n6. **NRI integration**: Hook points for resource plugins\n7. **Error semantics**: Distinguishes between \"not found\" and real errors\n\n---\n\n## 11. Key Files Cross-Reference\n\n### Kubernetes (CRI API Definition)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` - gRPC service definition\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.pb.go` - Generated protobuf code\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api_grpc.pb.go` - Generated gRPC code\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go` - Go interface definitions\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go` - Kubernetes CRI client\n\n### Containerd (CRI Implementation)\n- `plugins/cri/cri.go` - Plugin registration and gRPC server setup\n- `plugins/cri/runtime/plugin.go` - Runtime service plugin\n- `plugins/cri/images/plugin.go` - Image service plugin\n- `internal/cri/server/service.go` - Main criService struct\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go` - RunPodSandbox implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go` - StopPodSandbox implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go` - RemovePodSandbox implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/container_*.go` - Container operation implementations\n- `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go` - Instrumentation layer\n- `internal/cri/store/sandbox/` - Sandbox state management\n- `internal/cri/store/container/` - Container state management\n\n### Vendoring in Kubernetes\n- `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` - Full CRI API definitions\n- `vendor/github.com/containerd/` - Containerd API types\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI is a well-designed, language-agnostic interface that defines a contract between Kubernetes and container runtimes. Containerd's implementation demonstrates:\n\n1. **Correct semantics**: Implements idempotent operations as specified\n2. **Robust state management**: Uses stores and leases to prevent resource leaks\n3. **Graceful error handling**: Distinguishes between expected and unexpected errors\n4. **Extensibility**: Supports runtime selection, plugins (NRI), and event streaming\n5. **Observability**: Multi-layer instrumentation for debugging and monitoring\n\nThe interface contract is enforced through gRPC's strongly-typed message definitions, allowing Kubernetes and containerd to evolve independently while maintaining compatibility through the CRI protocol versioning system.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1975,"cache_read_input_tokens":80759,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1975},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"120fae7f-8c1a-478c-8561-fc8f42fe3d73","uuid":"4d4b10ea-8d29-4fcf-adaa-ed5ef591db74"}

The analysis spans both the Kubernetes and containerd repositories, mapping the interface contract to concrete implementation.\n\n---\n\n## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition\n\n### 1.1 Definition Location\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n\nThe Kubernetes project maintains the Container Runtime Interface as a protocol buffer specification with gRPC service definitions. This is the source of truth for all container runtime implementations.\n\n### 1.2 Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService\n\nThe CRI RuntimeService gRPC interface defines the following key RPC methods:\n\n#### Sandbox Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\nservice RuntimeService {\n    // Version returns the runtime name, runtime version, and runtime API version.\n    rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse) {}\n\n    // RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes must ensure\n    // the sandbox is in the ready state on success.\n    rpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // StopPodSandbox stops any running process that is part of the sandbox and\n    // reclaims network resources (e.g., IP addresses) allocated to the sandbox.\n    // If there are any running containers in the sandbox, they must be forcibly\n    // terminated. This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if all\n    // relevant resources have already been reclaimed.\n    rpc StopPodSandbox(StopPodSandboxRequest) returns (StopPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox. If there are any running containers\n    // in the sandbox, they must be forcibly terminated and removed.\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the sandbox has\n    // already been removed.\n    rpc RemovePodSandbox(RemovePodSandboxRequest) returns (RemovePodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStatus returns the status of the PodSandbox. If the PodSandbox is\n    // not present, returns an error.\n    rpc PodSandboxStatus(PodSandboxStatusRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandbox returns a list of PodSandboxes.\n    rpc ListPodSandbox(ListPodSandboxRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n#### Container Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\n    // CreateContainer creates a new container in specified PodSandbox\n    rpc CreateContainer(CreateContainerRequest) returns (CreateContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StartContainer starts the container.\n    rpc StartContainer(StartContainerRequest) returns (StartContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StopContainer stops a running container with a grace period (i.e., timeout).\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the container has\n    // already been stopped.\n    rpc StopContainer(StopContainerRequest) returns (StopContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveContainer removes the container. If the container is running, the\n    // container must be forcibly removed.\n    rpc RemoveContainer(RemoveContainerRequest) returns (RemoveContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainers lists all containers by filters.\n    rpc ListContainers(ListContainersRequest) returns (ListContainersResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStatus returns status of the container. If the container is not\n    // present, returns an error.\n    rpc ContainerStatus(ContainerStatusRequest) returns (ContainerStatusResponse) {}\n```\n\n#### Advanced Operations\n```protobuf\n    // ExecSync runs a command in a container synchronously.\n    rpc ExecSync(ExecSyncRequest) returns (ExecSyncResponse) {}\n\n    // Exec prepares a streaming endpoint to execute a command in the container.\n    rpc Exec(ExecRequest) returns (ExecResponse) {}\n\n    // Attach prepares a streaming endpoint to attach to a running container.\n    rpc Attach(AttachRequest) returns (AttachResponse) {}\n\n    // PortForward prepares a streaming endpoint to forward ports from a PodSandbox.\n    rpc PortForward(PortForwardRequest) returns (PortForwardResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStats returns stats of the container.\n    rpc ContainerStats(ContainerStatsRequest) returns (ContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainerStats returns stats of all running containers.\n    rpc ListContainerStats(ListContainerStatsRequest) returns (ListContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandbox.\n    rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandboxes matching a filter.\n    rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // Status returns the status of the runtime.\n    rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse) {}\n\n    // GetContainerEvents gets container events from the CRI runtime\n    rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse) {}\n```\n\n### 1.3 ImageService gRPC Definition\n\nThe CRI also defines an ImageService interface:\n\n```protobuf\nservice ImageService {\n    // ListImages lists existing images.\n    rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageStatus returns the status of the image. If the image is not present,\n    // returns a response with ImageStatusResponse.Image set to nil.\n    rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n    rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveImage removes the image.\n    rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n    rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Message Type Hierarchy\n\nThe proto definitions include structured message types that form a clear contract:\n\n### Pod Sandbox Messages\n- `RunPodSandboxRequest` / `RunPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Contains `PodSandboxConfig` with metadata, network config, DNS, Linux config, etc.\n  - Returns the sandbox ID as a string\n- `StopPodSandboxRequest` / `StopPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `RemovePodSandboxRequest` / `RemovePodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `PodSandboxStatus` message contains:\n  - Sandbox ID, state, creation timestamp\n  - Network settings, metadata labels\n  - Linux-specific namespace paths\n\n### Container Messages\n- `CreateContainerRequest` / `CreateContainerResponse`\n- `StartContainerRequest` / `StartContainerResponse`\n- `ContainerStatus` contains state (created, running, exited) and detailed resource info\n\n---\n\n## 3. Generated gRPC Code\n\n### 3.1 gRPC Compilation\nThe proto files are compiled to generate:\n- **File**: `api_grpc.pb.go` - Contains the gRPC service definitions\n- Generated client interface: `RuntimeServiceClient`\n- Generated server interface: `RuntimeServiceServer`\n- Method handlers and registration functions\n\n### 3.2 Server Interface Example\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n    PodSandboxStatus(context.Context, *PodSandboxStatusRequest) (*PodSandboxStatusResponse, error)\n    // ... other methods\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Registration Function\n```go\nfunc RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s grpc.ServiceRegistrar, srv RuntimeServiceServer) {\n    // Registers all RPC handlers with the gRPC server\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### 4.1 Entry Point: CRI Plugin Registration\n\n**File**: `plugins/cri/cri.go` (containerd repository)\n\nThe containerd CRI plugin is initialized as a gRPC plugin:\n\n```go\nfunc init() {\n    defaultConfig := criconfig.DefaultServerConfig()\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,      // Runtime service\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,      // Sandbox controller\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,          // Node Resource Interface\n            plugins.EventPlugin,\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,\n        },\n        InitFn: initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 gRPC Server Implementation\n\n**Type**: `criGRPCServer` struct\n\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Embedded interface implementation\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer    // Embedded interface implementation\n    io.Closer\n    initializer                   // IsInitialized() method\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nThis structure:\n- **Embeds** the gRPC server interfaces from the CRI API\n- **Wraps** them with instrumentation for logging, metrics, and tracing\n- **Registers** both services with the gRPC server\n\n### 4.3 Service Implementation Layer\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe actual implementation is in the `criService` struct:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    RuntimeService    // Embedded dependency\n    ImageService      // Embedded dependency\n\n    // State management\n    config             criconfig.Config\n    sandboxStore       *sandboxstore.Store    // Stores pod sandbox metadata\n    containerStore     *containerstore.Store  // Stores container metadata\n    sandboxNameIndex   *registrar.Registrar   // Ensures unique names\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n\n    // Network and streaming\n    netPlugin          map[string]cni.CNI    // CNI plugin for networking\n    streamServer       streaming.Server      // For exec/attach streams\n\n    // Monitoring and integration\n    eventMonitor       *events.EventMonitor  // Container event tracking\n    nri                *nri.API              // Node Resource Interface\n    sandboxService     sandboxService        // Sandbox controller\n    runtimeHandlers    map[string]*runtime.RuntimeHandler\n    statsCollector     *StatsCollector\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 Method Implementation Example: RunPodSandbox\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and reserve name to prevent concurrent creation\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    metadata := config.GetMetadata()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n\n    if err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name: %w\", err)\n    }\n    defer func() {\n        if retErr != nil {\n            c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(name)\n        }\n    }()\n\n    // 2. Create lease for resource tracking\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    ls, err := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create lease: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Select OCI runtime based on config and runtime handler\n    ociRuntime, err := c.config.GetSandboxRuntime(config, r.GetRuntimeHandler())\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to get OCI runtime: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 4. Create sandbox store entry\n    sandbox := sandboxstore.NewSandbox(\n        sandboxstore.Metadata{\n            ID:             id,\n            Name:           name,\n            Config:         config,\n            RuntimeHandler: r.GetRuntimeHandler(),\n        },\n        sandboxstore.Status{\n            State: sandboxstore.StateUnknown,\n        },\n    )\n\n    // 5. Set up networking (CNI)\n    // 6. Start the sandbox via sandbox controller\n    // 7. Trigger NRI hooks for Node Resource Interface\n\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{\n        PodSandboxId: id,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Patterns:\n- **Resource isolation**: Each sandbox gets a lease for resource cleanup\n- **Name reservation**: Prevents concurrent creation of same sandbox\n- **Store management**: Maintains metadata in `sandboxStore` for lifecycle tracking\n- **Error recovery**: Deferred cleanup functions ensure partial failures are rolled back\n- **Instrumentation**: Wrapped with tracing spans and logging\n\n### 4.5 StopPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Look up sandbox in store (idempotent - returns success if not found)\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            // Idempotent: already stopped/removed, return success\n            return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error finding sandbox: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 2. Stop all containers in the sandbox (forced termination)\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.stopContainerRetryOnConnectionClosed(ctx, container, 0); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Stop the sandbox container itself if running or unknown\n    state := sandbox.Status.Get().State\n    if state == sandboxstore.StateReady || state == sandboxstore.StateUnknown {\n        if err := c.sandboxService.StopSandbox(ctx, sandbox.Sandboxer, sandbox.ID); err != nil {\n            if !errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop sandbox: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 4. Trigger NRI hooks\n    // 5. Update sandbox state to \"NotReady\"\n\n    return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Points:\n- **Idempotent semantics**: Returns success even if sandbox already stopped\n- **Cascading shutdown**: Stops all containers first, then the sandbox\n- **State tracking**: Uses internal state to avoid redundant operations\n- **Error handling**: Distinguishes between \"not found\" (ok) and real errors\n\n### 4.6 RemovePodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Find the sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // 2. Force-remove all containers in the sandbox\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.removeContainer(ctx, container.ID); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to remove container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Trigger NRI removal hooks\n    // 4. Release the sandbox name from the index\n    // 5. Delete lease\n    // 6. Remove from sandbox store\n\n    return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Instrumentation Layer\n\n### 5.1 Middleware Pattern\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\nContainerd wraps the criService with an instrumented service that adds:\n\n```go\ntype instrumentedService struct {\n    c runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Wrapped service\n}\n\nfunc (in *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Check if service is initialized\n    if err := in.checkInitialized(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // Log the request\n    log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox for %+v\", r.GetConfig().GetMetadata())\n\n    // Call the actual implementation\n    res, err := in.c.RunPodSandbox(ctx, r)\n\n    // Log the response or error\n    if err != nil {\n        log.G(ctx).WithError(err).Errorf(\"RunPodSandbox failed\")\n    } else {\n        log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox returns sandbox id %q\", res.GetPodSandboxId())\n    }\n\n    return res, err\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern provides:\n- **Logging**: Detailed request/response logging\n- **Metrics**: Request timing and counts\n- **Tracing**: Distributed tracing spans\n- **Validation**: Server initialization checks\n\n---\n\n## 6. Kubernetes Vendoring of Containerd APIs\n\n### 6.1 Vendor Structure\n\n**Location**: `vendor/github.com/containerd/` (in kubernetes repo)\n\nKubernetes vendors only the **API types** from containerd, not the full implementation:\n\n```\nvendor/github.com/containerd/\n├── containerd/\n│   └── api/\n│       ├── services/      # gRPC service definitions\n│       └── types/         # Common data types\n├── errdefs/              # Error definitions\n├── log/                  # Logging interface\n├── ttrpc/               # ttrpc protocol implementation\n└── typeurl/             # Type URL registry for protobuf\n```\n\n### 6.2 Key Vendored Components\n\n**containerd/api/types**: Core container and sandbox types that represent the container runtime state\n\n**containerd/errdefs**: Error codes that containerd uses:\n- `IsNotFound(err)` - checks if resource doesn't exist\n- `IsAlreadyExists(err)` - resource creation collision\n- `IsInvalidArgument(err)` - malformed request\n- `IsFailedPrecondition(err)` - resource in wrong state\n\nThis error package is critical for the idempotent semantics of CRI operations.\n\n### 6.3 Kubernetes CRI Client\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`\n\nKubernetes implements a client that communicates with containerd via the CRI interface:\n\n```go\ntype remoteRuntimeService struct {\n    runtimeClient runtimeapi.RuntimeServiceClient  // gRPC client\n    timeout       time.Duration\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig, runtimeHandler string) (string, error) {\n\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    resp, err := r.runtimeClient.RunPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.RunPodSandboxRequest{\n        Config:         config,\n        RuntimeHandler: runtimeHandler,\n    })\n\n    if err != nil {\n        return \"\", err\n    }\n\n    return resp.PodSandboxId, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, podSandBoxID string) error {\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    _, err := r.runtimeClient.StopPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.StopPodSandboxRequest{\n        PodSandboxId: podSandBoxID,\n    })\n\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Interface Contract and Semantics\n\n### 7.1 Idempotent Operations\n\nBoth `StopPodSandbox` and `RemovePodSandbox` are **idempotent**:\n- Multiple calls with same ID should succeed\n- Calling on non-existent resource should return success\n- Kubelet relies on this for reliable cleanup\n\n**Implementation guarantee**: In both containerd and Kubernetes client:\n```\nif err != nil && !isNotFound(err) {\n    return err\n}\n// Return success regardless\n```\n\n### 7.2 Cascading Lifecycle\n\nThe CRI defines a specific lifecycle:\n1. **RunPodSandbox** - Creates and starts sandbox (must be Ready)\n2. **CreateContainer** - Creates containers in the sandbox\n3. **StartContainer** - Starts the containers\n4. **StopContainer** - Stops containers gracefully\n5. **StopPodSandbox** - Stops sandbox (must terminate all containers)\n6. **RemoveContainer** - Removes container metadata\n7. **RemovePodSandbox** - Removes sandbox metadata\n\nContainerd enforces this through state tracking and cascading cleanup.\n\n### 7.3 Graceful vs Forced Termination\n\n- **StopContainer(grace_period)**: Sends SIGTERM, waits for grace period, then SIGKILL\n- **StopPodSandbox**: Forcibly terminates all containers (grace period = 0)\n- **RemovePodSandbox**: Forcibly removes all containers\n\n### 7.4 Resource Cleanup\n\nThree levels of resource management:\n1. **Leases** (containerd): Automatic cleanup of orphaned resources\n2. **Stores** (criService): In-memory tracking of sandbox/container metadata\n3. **CNI plugins**: Network namespace cleanup on sandbox removal\n\n---\n\n## 8. Message Flow Example: Create and Run Pod\n\n### Complete Request-Response Chain\n\n```\nKubelet Requests:\n1. RunPodSandbox(config)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.RunPodSandbox()\n   → Creates lease, reserves name, creates sandbox store entry\n   → Calls sandboxService.StartSandbox() with OCI runtime\n   → Returns sandbox_id\n   Response: RunPodSandboxResponse { pod_sandbox_id = \"abc123\" }\n\n2. CreateContainer(sandbox_id, config)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.CreateContainer()\n   → Creates container store entry\n   → Generates OCI spec from config\n   Response: CreateContainerResponse { container_id = \"def456\" }\n\n3. StartContainer(container_id)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.StartContainer()\n   → Calls sandboxService.StartTask() to run OCI runtime\n   Response: StartContainerResponse {}\n\n4. PodSandboxStatus(sandbox_id)\n   → gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   → criService.PodSandboxStatus()\n   → Returns sandbox state from store\n   Response: PodSandboxStatusResponse { status = SANDBOX_READY, ... }\n\nLater for cleanup:\n5. StopContainer(container_id, grace_period)\n   → Sends SIGTERM, waits, then SIGKILL\n   Response: StopContainerResponse {}\n\n6. RemoveContainer(container_id)\n   Response: RemoveContainerResponse {}\n\n7. StopPodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   → Stops all containers in sandbox\n   → Stops sandbox container\n   Response: StopPodSandboxResponse {}\n\n8. RemovePodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   → Removes all containers\n   → Releases name reservation\n   → Deletes lease\n   → Removes from store\n   Response: RemovePodSandboxResponse {}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Error Handling\n\n### 9.1 Error Types from Kubernetes CRI Spec\n\nAll operations return gRPC errors that map to error codes:\n- `Unimplemented` - Method not supported\n- `Internal` - Unexpected runtime error\n- `InvalidArgument` - Bad request parameters\n- `AlreadyExists` - Resource already created\n- `NotFound` - Resource doesn't exist\n- `FailedPrecondition` - Resource in wrong state\n\n### 9.2 Idempotency Handling\n\nContainerd's idempotent error handling:\n```go\n// In StopPodSandbox\nsandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(id)\nif err != nil {\n    if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n        return &StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil  // Success even if not found\n    }\n    return nil, err  // Real error\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Architecture Summary\n\n### 10.1 Layered Design\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ Kubernetes kubelet                              │\n│ (CRI client - runtime.RuntimeServiceClient)     │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │ gRPC calls over Unix socket\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ Containerd CRI Plugin (plugins/cri/cri.go)      │\n│ ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐   │\n│ │ criGRPCServer                            │   │\n│ │ - Embeds RuntimeServiceServer            │   │\n│ │ - Embeds ImageServiceServer              │   │\n│ └──────────────────────────────────────────┘   │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ Instrumentation Layer (internal/cri/instrument) │\n│ - Logging, metrics, tracing                     │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ criService Implementation                       │\n│ - sandbox_run.go: RunPodSandbox                 │\n│ - sandbox_stop.go: StopPodSandbox               │\n│ - sandbox_remove.go: RemovePodSandbox           │\n│ - container_*.go: Container operations          │\n└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘\n                   │\n┌──────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐\n│ Internal Services                               │\n│ - sandboxStore: State management                │\n│ - containerStore: Container tracking            │\n│ - sandboxService: Sandbox controller (runc)    │\n│ - streamServer: Exec/attach streaming           │\n│ - eventMonitor: Container event tracking        │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### 10.2 Key Design Principles\n\n1. **Interface-based abstraction**: CRI defines the contract, containerd implements it\n2. **Idempotent semantics**: Operations can be safely retried\n3. **Resource tracking**: Leases and stores manage resource lifecycle\n4. **State management**: Internal state prevents race conditions\n5. **Instrumentation**: Logging, metrics, and tracing at multiple layers\n6. **NRI integration**: Hook points for resource plugins\n7. **Error semantics**: Distinguishes between \"not found\" and real errors\n\n---\n\n## 11. Key Files Cross-Reference\n\n### Kubernetes (CRI API Definition)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` - gRPC service definition\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.pb.go` - Generated protobuf code\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api_grpc.pb.go` - Generated gRPC code\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go` - Go interface definitions\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go` - Kubernetes CRI client\n\n### Containerd (CRI Implementation)\n- `plugins/cri/cri.go` - Plugin registration and gRPC server setup\n- `plugins/cri/runtime/plugin.go` - Runtime service plugin\n- `plugins/cri/images/plugin.go` - Image service plugin\n- `internal/cri/server/service.go` - Main criService struct\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go` - RunPodSandbox implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go` - StopPodSandbox implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go` - RemovePodSandbox implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/container_*.go` - Container operation implementations\n- `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go` - Instrumentation layer\n- `internal/cri/store/sandbox/` - Sandbox state management\n- `internal/cri/store/container/` - Container state management\n\n### Vendoring in Kubernetes\n- `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` - Full CRI API definitions\n- `vendor/github.com/containerd/` - Containerd API types\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI is a well-designed, language-agnostic interface that defines a contract between Kubernetes and container runtimes. Containerd's implementation demonstrates:\n\n1. **Correct semantics**: Implements idempotent operations as specified\n2. **Robust state management**: Uses stores and leases to prevent resource leaks\n3. **Graceful error handling**: Distinguishes between expected and unexpected errors\n4. **Extensibility**: Supports runtime selection, plugins (NRI), and event streaming\n5. **Observability**: Multi-layer instrumentation for debugging and monitoring\n\nThe interface contract is enforced through gRPC's strongly-typed message definitions, allowing Kubernetes and containerd to evolve independently while maintaining compatibility through the CRI protocol versioning system.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
